   var ajax = new Array();
		function TrackClick(link,title) {

			var index = ajax.length;
			ajax[index] = new sack();		
			ajax[index].requestFile = "http://www.mymirrorworld.com?wp_click_tracked="+link+"***"+title+"***";	
			ajax[index].onCompletion = null;

			//FireFox 3 is a bitch; it doesn't track links which open in "self"
			var onunload_ran = 0;
			window.onunload = function () {
				onunload_ran = 1;
				ajax[index].runAJAX();
			}

			if(onunload_ran == 0){
				ajax[index].runAJAX();
			}

			return true;
		}

    <article class="post-15636 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-fashion" id="post-15636">
     <div class="post-header">
      <span class="cat">
       <a href="http://www.mymirrorworld.com/category/fashion/" title="View all posts in Fashion">
        Fashion
       </a>
      </span>
      <h1>
       Fashion Inspriration  Meine Statementketten
      </h1>
      <span class="date">
       30. Januar 2015
      </span>
     </div>
     <div class="post-image">
      <a href="http://www.mymirrorworld.com/2015/01/statementketten/">
       <img alt="Meine Statementketten 2" class="attachment-full-thumb wp-post-image" height="814" src="http://www.mymirrorworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Meine-Statementketten-2.jpg" width="700"/>
      </a>
     </div>
     <div class="post-entry">
      <input class="jpibfi" type="hidden"/>
      <p style="text-align: justify;">
       Statementketten haben sich inzwischen schon richtig etabliert und sind mittlerweile auch in fast jedem Shop erhltlich. Ich muss ja gestehen, dass ich ganz am Anfang kein groer Freund der aufflligen Ketten war, weil ich einfach nicht wusste, wie ich sie kombinieren soll, ohne wie ein Christbaum auszusehen. Inzwischen mag ich die Schmuckstcke aber richtig gerne, denn kaum etwas, wertet ein schlichtes Outfit schneller auf, als eine solche Kette. In meiner Schmucklade befinden sich derzeit 5 Statementketten. Nicht besonders viele, ich wei, aber ich bin mit meiner kleinen Sammlung zufrieden und wechsle gerne durch. Am liebsten trage ich meine Statementketten zu Blusen oder in letzter Zeit auch gerne zu Strickpullovern. Meine persnliche Kettenqueen ist brigens
       <a href="http://www.alliwantiseverything.at/2013/08/statment-necklaces-how-i-wear-them.html" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.alliwantiseverything.at/2013/08/statment-necklaces-how-i-wear-them.html', 'Steffi']);" target="_blank">
        Steffi
       </a>
       . Ich finde, keine kombiniert diese Schmuckstcke so gekonnt wie sie.
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: justify;">
       <span id="more-15636">
       </span>
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: justify;">
       Im Moment finden sich meiner Meinung nach wieder richtig hbsche Modelle in den Geschften, einige davon habe ich rausgesucht und auf meine imaginre Wunschliste gesetzt.
      </p>
      <p>
       <img alt="" border="0" height="792" id="Image-Maps-Com-image-maps-2015-01-30-023652" src="http://www.mymirrorworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/Statementkette.jpg" usemap="#image-maps-2015-01-30-023652" width="700"/>
      </p>
      <map id="ImageMapsCom-image-maps-2015-01-30-023652" name="image-maps-2015-01-30-023652">

      <p style="text-align: justify;">
       <a href="http://www.mymirrorworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/How-to-style-a-white-cotton-blouse-outfit-weie-baumwollbluse-3-3.jpg" onclick="return TrackClick('http%3A%2F%2Fwww.mymirrorworld.com%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2014%2F12%2FHow-to-style-a-white-cotton-blouse-outfit-wei%C3%9Fe-baumwollbluse-3-3.jpg','')">
        <img alt="How to style a white cotton blouse outfit weie baumwollbluse 3-3" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-15348" height="1054" onclick="return TrackClick('http%3A%2F%2Fwww.mymirrorworld.com%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2014%2F12%2FHow-to-style-a-white-cotton-blouse-outfit-wei%C3%9Fe-baumwollbluse-3-3.jpg','')" src="http://www.mymirrorworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/How-to-style-a-white-cotton-blouse-outfit-weie-baumwollbluse-3-3.jpg" width="700"/>
       </a>
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: center;">
       Bltenkette von H&amp;M. Msste aktuell noch in zwei Farben erhltlich sein.
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: justify;">
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: justify;">
       <a href="http://www.mymirrorworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/How-to-style-a-white-cotton-blouse-outfit-weie-baumwollbluse-2-1.jpg" onclick="return TrackClick('http%3A%2F%2Fwww.mymirrorworld.com%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2014%2F12%2FHow-to-style-a-white-cotton-blouse-outfit-wei%C3%9Fe-baumwollbluse-2-1.jpg','')">
        <img alt="How to style a white cotton blouse outfit weie baumwollbluse 2-1" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-15260" height="1054" onclick="return TrackClick('http%3A%2F%2Fwww.mymirrorworld.com%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2014%2F12%2FHow-to-style-a-white-cotton-blouse-outfit-wei%C3%9Fe-baumwollbluse-2-1.jpg','')" src="http://www.mymirrorworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/How-to-style-a-white-cotton-blouse-outfit-weie-baumwollbluse-2-1.jpg" width="700"/>
       </a>
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: center;">
       Groe Perlenkette via Ebay.
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: justify;">
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: justify;">
       <a href="http://www.mymirrorworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Herbstoutfit_Blog_10.jpg" onclick="return TrackClick('http%3A%2F%2Fwww.mymirrorworld.com%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2014%2F11%2FHerbstoutfit_Blog_10.jpg','')">
        <img alt="Herbstoutfit_Blog_10" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-14474" height="1054" onclick="return TrackClick('http%3A%2F%2Fwww.mymirrorworld.com%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2014%2F11%2FHerbstoutfit_Blog_10.jpg','')" src="http://www.mymirrorworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/11/Herbstoutfit_Blog_10.jpg" width="700"/>
       </a>
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: center;">
       Kette mit Perlen und Steinchen von OASAP.
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: justify;">
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: justify;">
       <a href="http://www.mymirrorworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/Guerlain-Exceptional-Complette-Lip-Colour-Rouge-G-820-2.jpg" onclick="return TrackClick('http%3A%2F%2Fwww.mymirrorworld.com%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2014%2F12%2FGuerlain-Exceptional-Complette-Lip-Colour-Rouge-G-820-2.jpg','')">
        <img alt="Guerlain Exceptional Complette Lip Colour Rouge G 820 2" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-15181" height="955" onclick="return TrackClick('http%3A%2F%2Fwww.mymirrorworld.com%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2014%2F12%2FGuerlain-Exceptional-Complette-Lip-Colour-Rouge-G-820-2.jpg','')" src="http://www.mymirrorworld.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/Guerlain-Exceptional-Complette-Lip-Colour-Rouge-G-820-2.jpg" width="700"/>
       </a>
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: center;">
       Blumenkette von Zara.
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: justify;">
      </p>
      <p style="text-align: justify;">
       Wie steht ihr zu Statementketten? Mgt ihr sie (noch)? Oder tragt ihr lieber kleinere, filligraneren Halsschmuck?
      </p>
      <h6 style="text-align: right;">
       Enthlt Affiliate-Links.
      </h6>

/*  Collapse Functions, version 2.0
 *
 *--------------------------------------------------------------------------*/
String.prototype.trim = function() {
  return this.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");
}

function createCookie(name,value,days) {
  if (days) {
    var date = new Date();
    date.setTime(date.getTime()+(days*24*60*60*1000));
    var expires = "; expires="+date.toGMTString();
  } else {
    var expires = "";
  }
  document.cookie = name+"="+value+expires+"; path=/";
}

function readCookie(name) {
  var nameEQ = name + "=";
  var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
  for(var i=0;i &lt; ca.length;i++) {
    var c = ca[i];
    while (c.charAt(0)==' ') {
      c = c.substring(1,c.length);
    }
    if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) {
      return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
    }
  }
  return null;
}

function eraseCookie(name) {
  createCookie(name,"",-1);
}

function addExpandCollapse(id, expandSym, collapseSym, accordion) {
  jQuery('#' + id + ' span.expand').live('click', function() {
    if (accordion==1) {
      var theDiv = jQuery(this).parent().parent().find('span.collapse').parent().children('div');
      jQuery(theDiv).hide('normal');
      jQuery(this).parent().parent().find('span.collapse').removeClass('collapse').addClass('expand');
      createCookie(theDiv.attr('id'), 0, 7);
      jQuery(this).parent().parent().find('span.sym').html(expandSym);
      //jQuery('#' + id + ' .expand .sym').html(expandSym);
    }
    expandArch(this, expandSym, collapseSym);
    return false;
  });
  jQuery('#' + id + ' span.collapse').live('click', function() {
    collapseArch(this, expandSym, collapseSym);
    return false;
  });
}

function expandArch(symbol, expandSym, collapseSym) {
    var theDiv = jQuery(symbol).parent().children('div');
    try {
      if (collapsItems[jQuery(theDiv).attr('id')]!='') {
        jQuery(theDiv).html(collapsItems[jQuery(theDiv).attr('id')]).show('normal');
      } else {
        jQuery(theDiv).show('normal');
      }
    } catch (err) {
      jQuery(theDiv).show('normal');
    }
    jQuery(symbol).removeClass('expand').addClass('collapse');
    jQuery(symbol).children('.sym').html(collapseSym);
  createCookie(theDiv.attr('id'), 1, 7);
}
function collapseArch(symbol, expandSym, collapseSym) {
    var theDiv = jQuery(symbol).parent().children('div');
    jQuery(theDiv).hide('normal');
    jQuery(symbol).removeClass('collapse').addClass('expand');
    jQuery(symbol).children('.sym').html(expandSym);
  createCookie(theDiv.attr('id'), 0, 7);
}
addExpandCollapse('widget-collapsarch-2-top','&#x25BA;', '&#x25BC;', 0)// ]]&gt;
       </script>
      </li>
     </ul>
